Helicopter blades undergo constant turbulence, far more than an airplane wings, yet they must be light, strong, and flexible. Not too far from what a fly rod has to put up with during a blitz of tuna. The US Army found that by making Apache blades from graphite composites with thermoplastic-enriched thermoset resins, the blades could produce a larger airfoil, rotate at higher speeds, and carry a bigger payload at the same time making it four times stronger!<br /><img width="200" height="114" align="right" alt="Orvis Zero Gravity" src="http://www.westbranchangler.com/images/ebay/Orvis_ZG/f-22.jpg" /></p><p>These composites are also used in the V-22 Osprey, C-17 transport planes, the F-22 fighterScientist who helped formuate the Zero G Fly Rod, the Joint Strike Fighter, and the top-secret UCAV (Unmanned Combat Aerial Vehicle). Our exclusive consultant on fly rod materials is a composite scientist with top security clearance. The new Zero G fly rods are a result of his research with the military and our testing of fly rods using this technology in the field.<br />What makes them so special?</p><p><span style="font-weight: bold;">Thermoplastic Resins</span></p><p>Only three fly rod series in the world exist that use high-cure thermoplastic enriched thermoset resins: Orvis Zero Gravity, Orvis T-3, and Orvis TLS Power Matrix. Our exclusive resins are set at a high cure temperature, and completely encase the graphite fibers used as the main source of power, distance, and accuracy in a fly rod. In contrast to the standard epoxy resins found in all other fly rods, thermoplastics make a fly rod stronger, tougher, and more accurate.</p><p><span style="font-weight: bold;">Boron Fibers in our Strategic Positioning System</span></p><p>Boron is a stiff, strong, and very expensive fiber. Alone, its too stiff to make a fly rod by conventional means. But, when we add just the right amount of boron into the butt section of a rod it produces a reserve power, because boron compresses less under stress. This power takes over in your longest casts or when playing big fish with maximum stress on the rod. Plus, our new Strategic Positioning System, developed specifically for Zero Gravity rods, allows us to place the boron fibers in precisely the right spot and in just the right amount for each individual rod taper.</p><p><span style="font-weight: bold;">Unidirectional Carbon Scrim</span></p><p><img width="200" height="102" align="left" alt="Orvis Zero Gravity" src="http://www.westbranchangler.com/images/ebay/Orvis_ZG/wrap.jpg" />Did you know fiberglass is used in most all other graphite rods?The Latest in Scrim Technology Graphite and resins by themselves dont offer enough strength to withstand normal fishing conditions. So, a supportive layer of fiberglass is attached to the graphite fibers before theyre wrapped around a steel mandrel to form the taper. Its worked well for 30 years, but it adds weight to a rod. Our Zero G rods use the latest in scrim technology: Unidirectional graphite scrim, which is lighter, stronger, and more dependable than fiberglass scrim. Because this material, part of our Strategic Positioning System, is so strong we only need to use a fraction of the graphite, as compared to the fiberglass used in other rods. The result is a much thinner rod yet even stronger fly rod.</p><p>Some other rod manufacturers claim to use graphite scrim in their rods, but many use a mat of graphite fibers, which doesnt offer the strength and superior fiber alignment (and thus better rod tracking you get by using unidirectional graphite scrim.</p><p><span style="font-weight: bold;">The Bottom Line:</span></p><p>Zero G rod blanks are 25% stronger yet 25% thinner than comparable blanks, and 40% lighter.<br />If youre totally satisfied with your casting, have no worries about your rod breaking on the trip of a lifetime, and can put the fly exactly where you want it every time, you probably dont need a Zero G. But, if youre not always happy with your casting, the Zero G technology is the best reason you will ever have to upgrade.</p></td></tr><tr><td>&nbsp;</td></tr><tr><td><div align="center" class="style3"></div><br /></td></tr><tr><td><div align="center" class="style3">Questions? WBROCLA	948	CLA REELS/SPOOLS	<table style="background-color: rgb(220, 220, 220);" align="center" border="0" cellpadding="3" cellspacing="1" width="90%"><tbody><tr><td colspan="2" class="reelschartsrowthree"><p>TheCLA has set a new standard for affordable, hybrid large arbor flyreels. This series incorporates a superior drag mechanism that isextraordinarily smooth, heat resistant and provides incredible stoppingpower. While the CLA is offered at a reasonable price, no designfeatures have been overlooked. Each reel in this series is designedwith a specific diameter and width to maximize the properties of dragconsistency and quick line retrieval. The CLA has become our dealers'"go to" reel for anglers that are looking for an American made, highquality, reasonably priced fly reel.</p> <p><span style="font-weight: bold;">CLA 4-7 (Larger Components for Bigger Fish!)</span><br>Themechanical design of all CLA reels is consistent throughout the series,but improvements have been made to the four largest sizes (4-7) tosupport their use in battling bigger fish. When comparing the largerCLA reels to the smaller sized 1, 1.5, 2 and 3 reels, you will findthat they have a larger sized drag knob, handle and spool cap, but mostimportantly, they have a STRONGER DRAG SYSTEM. To ensure smoothperformance with fast-running fish, the four larger sized CLA reelshave also been equipped with oil-impregnated bushings for improvedspool rotation. The frame and spool have been reinforced to eliminateflexing when battling heavyweights. With a wide range of sizesavailable, the CLA series is appropriate for any fishing application,including Spey.</p> </td>  </tr>  <tr>    <td class="reelschartsrowone"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Frame/Spool Material:</span></td>    <td class="reelschartsrowtwo">6061-T6 proprietary aluminum alloy</td>  </tr>    <tr>    <td class="reelschartsrowtwo"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Manufacturing Specifications:</span></td>    <td class="reelschartsrowone">Fully machined, 1 piece frame, 1 piece spool with a Delrin pressed hub - manufactured on automated CNC machining centers</td>  </tr>    <tr>    <td class="reelschartsrowone"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Drag Material:</span></td>    <td class="reelschartsrowtwo">Delrin 500AF with impregnated Teflon - space-age polymer that is durable, heat resistant, self lubricating and maintenance free</td>  </tr>    <tr>    <td class="reelschartsrowtwo"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Drag Mechanism:</span></td>    <td class="reelschartsrowone">Delrin 500AF to anodized aluminum interface - push frame friction disc drag system</td>  </tr>    <tr>    <td class="reelschartsrowone"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Drag Engagement System:</span></td>    <td class="reelschartsrowtwo">Redundancy radial pawl engagement</td>  </tr>    <tr>    <td class="reelschartsrowtwo"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Spool Rotation Mechanism:</span></td>    <td class="reelschartsrowone">Delrinhub rotating on a stainless steel spindle, oil impregnated bronzebushings rotating on a stainless steel spindle (Sizes 4-7)</td>  </tr>    <tr>    <td class="reelschartsrowone"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Number of Reels in Series:</span></td>    <td class="reelschartsrowtwo">Eight</td>  </tr>    <tr>    <td class="reelschartsrowtwo"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Fly Rod Coverage:</span></td>    <td class="reelschartsrowone">2 wt. - 13 wt. WBROMTM	951	MOMENTUM FLY REEL/SPOOL	<table style="background-color: rgb(220, 220, 220);" align="center" border="0" cellpadding="3" cellspacing="1" width="90%"><tbody><tr><td colspan="2" class="reelschartsrowthree"><p><span style="font-weight: bold; font-style: italic;"><span style="color: black;">Mo men tum: (mO-'men-tm) (n. pl.)</span> - A measure of the motion of a body equal to the product of its mass and velocity.</span></p> <p><span style="font-weight: bold; font-style: italic;"><span style="color: black;">Synonyms:</span> drive, energy, power, strength</span></p>   <p>TheMomentum reel series has proven to be the strongest and most dependablesaltwater fly reel on the water today, and is a perfect example of howto maximize the benefits of carbon fiber technology in a drag system.Stiffness, strength, heat resistance, shock-dampening capabilities andinfinite fatigue resistance are all properties of carbon fiber thathelp make the Momentum drag system the strongest and most dependablebig game reel available. We have partnered with Kestrel Bike Company inthe development of the Momentum's carbon fiber drag system. Our vastexperience in fly reel design and manufacturing is equally matched byKestrel's expertise in the design and production of carbon fibercomponents. Kestrel has been manufacturing the world's finest carbonfiber bikes since 1987. In fact, Kestrel designed and produced the veryfirst all-carbon bike frame. They are pioneers in the carbon fiberindustry and we were thrilled that a company of their caliber agreed tojoin us in the development of this new drag technology. When it comesto engineering, development and production of carbon fiber products,Kestrel has written the book and their expertise with carbon fiber issimply unmatched.</p> <p>Welcome to the next generation of Rossproducts! The Momentum series represents a cosmic departure fromcurrent Ross designs in both function and style. The carbon fiber wehave employed for the Momentum drag system is incredibly strong! Themeasurement of the strength for this material is "ksi", which denotestensile strength in thousands of pounds per square inch. So just howstrong is our carbon fiber drag system? To get a good perspective onthis, the aluminum used to produce Ross products is 45ksi; meaning itcan resist a tension load of 45,000 pounds per square inch of material.This is pretty impressive until you realize that the carbon fiber usedin the Momentum drag system is 700ksi - vastly stronger than aluminum,steel and even titanium!</p> <p>The first time you handle a Momentumreel, you will be amazed with its meticulous machining and ergonomicdesign. We have custom fit this series with a large, well positioneddrag knob - easily found for adjustment during the heat of battle, butnever in the way. Additionally, the Momentum's handle has been designedto fit comfortably between your fingers, but will never slip free whentaking on a monster fish. Each reel in this series is designed with aspecific diameter and width to maximize the properties of dragconsistency and quick line retrieval. With 6.3 square inches ofeffective drag surface, and 12 pounds of dead lift weight, the Momentumseries has three times the effective stopping power of every dragtested. Put simply, the Momentum is the strongest fly fishing reel onthe market today; and it costs considerably less than many competitivebrands. A triple redundancy drag system ensures dependability under themost demanding fishing conditions, and by adding in features liketitanium drag components, a quick-release locking spool and watershedding grooves on the palming rim, you have the ultimate big game flyreel. With a wide range of sizes available, the Momentum series isappropriate for any fishing application, including Spey.</p> </td>  </tr>  <tr>    <td class="reelschartsrowone"><span WBHHHRKE	1070	GLADSTONE BAMBOO FLY RODS	  <h1 class="style1">GLADSTONE (SPLIT BAMBOO)  </h1>  <p><span class="col">Namedin tribute to Callum Gladstone, our master-builder of split-bamboo flyrods, the first thing that you will notice about this new rod is itsspectacular appearance. Prior to the building process, the finestTonkin bamboo is hand-flamed, resulting in a rich, dark browntortoiseshell finish.<br>      <br> This two-piece rod series isavailable in three sizes, each with its own individual taper thatcelebrates the achievements of some of the greatest American split-canerod builders of the past: the Leonard family, Everett Garrison andEdward Payne. Minute adjustments are made to the Hardy precisionplanning form, to painstakingly recreate a modern version of theseclassic tapers. The perfect angle and taper on each spline means thatthe finished rod forms a perfect hexagon. Each rod shares in common theâ€˜swelled buttâ€™ that contributes considerable backbone to the feel,allowing a deep action to be combined with excellent dampeningcharacteristics.</span>    </p><p> The all new series features a Carbon Fiber Composite disc drag system and V-Arbor design. The patented, seamless engagement drag is sealed, however is serviceable if required. The Rogue uses four sealed precision stainless steel ball bearings, with no plastic parts or bushings. <br><br>The distinctive V-Arbor design maintains a larger effective diameter for the portion of the fly line and backing that is actually used when fishing. The balance of the backing is stored in the V bottom of the arbor, always available when needed. <br><br>The Rogue has a Stealth Black polished finish with optional spool colors.
